patch = {} as Record<string, null | undefined | Partial<Data>>
    snap_id = 0
    @ $mol_mem_key patch_snap(id: number) {
        sleep(100)
        this.snap_id++
        const patch = this.patch
        this.patch = {}
        return patch
    }

    @action snap_id_get() { return this.snap_id }

    @ $mol_mem_key
    value(id: string, next?: Data) {
        this.patch[id] = next
        const patch = this.patch_snap(this.snap_id_get())

        return this.values(Object.keys(patch), patch)[id]
    }
